View Profile Those amazing marshmallow Peeps Share Tweet Pin Share Stumble Tumble Saved Marshmallow Peeps are Easter basket staples that have been around for decades. However, people do more than eat Peeps — they also use them to create cool (and often hilarious) art. Those amazing marshmallow Peeps Peeps dioramas Marshmallow Peeps are Easter basket staples that have been around for decades. However, people do more than eat Peeps — they also use them to create cool (and often hilarious) art. Peeps diorama contests are embraced by people all over the country, with many newspapers and other organizations sponsoring annual contests, including The Denver Post, Fort Worth Star-Telegram, St. Paul Pioneer Press, The Washington Post, and even the American Bar Association Journal. A few of our favorite Peeps dioramas from the last few years follow. You can visit the Peeps website to find details on all the contests. OccuPeep D.C. Peeps get political! Created by Cori E. Wright of Crystal City, Virginia, this Peeps diorama was selected as the winner of The Washington Post's Sixth Annual Peeps Diorama Contest held in 2012. Photo credit: rbasallote via Flickr, CC BY-NC-ND 2.0 Sesame Peep All fans of Sesame Street (Isn't that everyone?) will love this Peeps diorama. Created in 2008 and entered in the Washington Post's Peep Show II contest, this diorama is one of our favorites from the talented and creative MaryLea Harris. Check out her blog, Pink and Green Mama. Photo credit: MaryLea Harris, Pink and Green Mama Octopeep Octopeep gave birth in 2009 as a tribute to Nadya Suleman — Octomom. You have to love the detail on this one, from the baby Peeps' blankets to the surgical masks. Photo credit: Joe Loongvia via Flickr, CC BY-SA 2.0 Village Peeps Everyone sings along to "YMCA" with the Village Peeps. This diorama was entered in the 2009 St. Paul Pioneer Press Marshmallow Peeps Diorama Contest. Photo credit: Joe Loongvia via Flickr, CC BY-SA 2.0 Goodnight, Peep In 2010, Pink and Green Mama's MaryLea Harris entered this colorful and detailed Peeps diorama in The Washington Post Peep Show IV contest, where she was selected as a finalist. Photo credit: MaryLea Harris, Pink and Green Mama Peeps yoga Everyone is into yoga these days — even the Peeps. This Peeps yoga diorama was one of the entries in last year's St. Paul Pioneer Press contest. Photo credit: Joel Homme The Voice of Peeps Peep Shelton, Peep Aguilera, Peep Green and Peep Levine got together to form the Peeps version of NBC's The Voice. This Peeps diorama was another entry in the St. Paul Pioneer Press contest. Photo credit: Megan and Dana Lowell, Jessica Doody Peeps gone wrong When left alone, the psycho Peeps can take over. Photo credit: Pirate Alicevia via Flickr, CC BY-SA 2.0 More about Easter Bunny-approved Easter decor tips 3 Fun DIY Easter centerpieces Pretty Easter decorating ideas Break away from eggs: Tasty Easter treats Funny bunny: How to fold Easter bunny napkins Tagged in crafts easter Recommended for You Comments Related Articles Hot New in Holidays & Seasons Close The menu button now contains all of the sections of our site.
